## <a name="windows-server-2003-r2-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="3ded5-704">Attributi di Windows Server 2003 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3ded5-704">Windows Server 2003 R2 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3ded5-705">Questa classe contiene gli attributi seguenti per Windows Server 2003 R2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3ded5-705">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2003 R2:</span></span>
